  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_161e586a-2293-4b18-8124-418dbccb65cd'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText14572909115500608924" style="display:none">Marissa is a craps dealer, and in one quick second that she never wants to remember, her life turns to crap. Her best friend convinces her that the cure for a breakup is a hookup, and reluctantly, she heeds this advice.<br /><br />However, Jack (what was his name again?) is not the average girl's revenge sex.<br /><br />Jack is a celebrity in his niche of the music world. Women throw themselves at him, toss their lingerie on the stage, and scream his name. Marissa has no idea of his public identity, and while she does not initially throw herself at him, she does go on to toss aside her lingerie and ultimately scream his name.<br /><br />Five minutes after parting, Marissa holds no illusions about seeing him again, but does vow a new outlook on her life and herself.<br /><br />Five days later, they exchange a very short text. <br /><br />Five months later, Jack astounds her with an invitation to Los Angeles. Although Jack is now a star in her very non rock star fantasies, Marissa is concealing a huge secret that prevents her from accepting. <br /><br />Five years later, the secret comes out and despite the conflicting emotions each feels towards the another, they must meld their two worlds together.</span>

<div id="review_713646241" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/713646241" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/713646241?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer713646241" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13661132632840080331">An easy 4 stars for a different type of rock star romance.<br/><br/>When Marissa attends a rock festival with her best friend Olivia, she knew the friends plans were to help her friend get over her ex by crawling in bed with a new man. But when Olivia leaves with the first roadie that catches her eye, Marissa finds herself in a situation that leads to meeting Jack Storm. Lead singer of Jackal. She had no idea who he is, but there is an instant attraction that leads to a couple of romps before they part.<br/><br/>It</span>
  <span id="freeText13661132632840080331" style="display:none">An easy 4 stars for a different type of rock star romance.<br /><br />When Marissa attends a rock festival with her best friend Olivia, she knew the friends plans were to help her friend get over her ex by crawling in bed with a new man. But when Olivia leaves with the first roadie that catches her eye, Marissa finds herself in a situation that leads to meeting Jack Storm. Lead singer of Jackal. She had no idea who he is, but there is an instant attraction that leads to a couple of romps before they part.<br /><br />It isn't until five years passes that a situation arises that requires her to reach out to him. Seeking help and in turn revealing the secret that kept her from accepting his invitation years ago to see him again. Although the secret is not a hard one to guess, I'll let you discover that on your own. <br /><br />With Marissa and Jack forced back into each others lives, the connection they shared that one afternoon is still there. But there is far too many issues with what she never told him and issues with communication that leave these two constantly getting their signals crossed.<br /><br />Jack Who? turned out to be an unexpected surprise. I had this downloaded, but yet I couldn't figure out just where I got it from. So I thought, what the hell. Let's give this one a go. It was a very cute romance and although a bit predictable with the "secret" was still a great romance. It didn't have the angst that comes with some rock star books, although I think that might come with book two. The story sticks close to Marissa's home - away from the glam of LA and the doubts that will surely be part of the lifestyle she is going to have to eventually see first hand. <br /><br />Jack was a complete sweetie-pie and never really gives you any concerns over what kind of guy he was. And although Marissa seemed to be focused on playing games to get what she wanted, she didn't seem to hang on to those notions for too long after seeing first hand that this just made things far more complex.<br /><br />The only issue I found was a bit in the transitions between scenes. There were moments that didn't flow into the other, that caused me to pause and go back to read the prior few lines to see if I missed something. Drifting from thoughts to actions it was hard to make that leap in certain points, but it wasn't so much to deter from the story. <br /><br />I look forward to seeing what happens in the next book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13661132632840080331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2032716523" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2032716523" />
    <a title="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog"><img alt="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514480818p2/3243151.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2032716523?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ " href="/user/show/3243151-bianca-bj-s-book-blog">✰ Bianca ✰ BJ&#39;s Book Blog ✰ </a>

I loved writing this book on wattpad. It was like a party as each chapter went up. There would be guesses about what these two crazy characters would do next, and ideas would take shape for the next chapter. The input from readers chapter to chapter was invaluable. <div id="review_718729854" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718729854" />
    <a title="J.J. Ellis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2129130-j-j-ellis"><img alt="J.J. Ellis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442878491p2/2129130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718729854?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J.J. Ellis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J.J. Ellis" href="/user/show/2129130-j-j-ellis">J.J. Ellis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718729854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14062824018384086762">When I first 'picked up' Jack Who, I expected to enjoy it. But boy oh boy I didn't know how much I would enjoy it. To start out, who doesn't love a story about a sexy rock star! Within my first reading session, I squealed aloud like a teenager, got goosebumps, and felt tears in my eyes. I love it when a books starts out like that! Also within the first reading session I fell madly in love with Jack and Marissa and just when I thought I knew what would happen the author surprised me. I love it wh</span>
  <span id="freeText14062824018384086762" style="display:none">When I first 'picked up' Jack Who, I expected to enjoy it. But boy oh boy I didn't know how much I would enjoy it. To start out, who doesn't love a story about a sexy rock star! Within my first reading session, I squealed aloud like a teenager, got goosebumps, and felt tears in my eyes. I love it when a books starts out like that! Also within the first reading session I fell madly in love with Jack and Marissa and just when I thought I knew what would happen the author surprised me. I love it when that happens!<br /><br />Truthfully I think this story is one that every teenaged girl dreams about. Falling in love with a rock star!!! Okay, I'm not 100 % sure other girls feel this way, but I know I sure did! I wanted to grow up to be a rock star's lover. And you know, I got to live that dream through this book. Great writing, awesome character development and a tremendous story come together in a book that I will never forget. And as I get older and want to experience some nostalgia I can go back and read Jack Who and relive my teen years.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14062824018384086762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_736564321" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/736564321" />
    <a title="Melissa Lucas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22661526-melissa-lucas"><img alt="Melissa Lucas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1382414141p2/22661526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/736564321?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa Lucas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa Lucas" href="/user/show/22661526-melissa-lucas">Melissa Lucas</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer736564321" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14421520221790838654">I think I can honestly say I have never read a romance novel based around rock stars and I am kicking myself for not doing so sooner. <br/><br/>Jack Who was a fantastic read from beginning to end, I loved Marissa and Jack, their story was very heart warming and Tristan was so adorable, I especially enjoyed Jack's scenes with Tristan, they pulled at my heartstrings in a good way. Marissa was a great main character, she had her flaws, especially when it came to Jack Storm, but she learns to deal with her in</span>
  <span id="freeText14421520221790838654" style="display:none">I think I can honestly say I have never read a romance novel based around rock stars and I am kicking myself for not doing so sooner. <br /><br />Jack Who was a fantastic read from beginning to end, I loved Marissa and Jack, their story was very heart warming and Tristan was so adorable, I especially enjoyed Jack's scenes with Tristan, they pulled at my heartstrings in a good way. Marissa was a great main character, she had her flaws, especially when it came to Jack Storm, but she learns to deal with her insecurities with some help from the gorgeous rock star and her loving family and friends.<br /><br />Lisa has written an amazing novel and I am keen to start reading the next book so I can continue Jack and Marissa's journey. For all those out there who are looking for a Rock star in their life, Jack Storm is just the man for you! I would definitely recommend this to everyone I know.</span>

  <span id="freeText15515584221780172154" style="display:none">Jack Who?: Perfect Storms (Silver Strings G, #1) by Lisa Gillis is an exceptional romantic novel full or even bursting with passion in every delicious chapter. The author has mastered this well overdone genre and given it a firm kick in the pants lingerie-wise and come up with a superb winner. I so loved this book with its well-written dialog, catchy theme of girl meets rock star, lusts for rock star, beds rock star then ....<br />Marissa falls head over high heels in lust for Jack St .... who? Almost gave that away. But she doesn't know how to handle a major babe attractor especially a megastar rocker. As will often happen the affair fizzles out .... or does it. The story spans five years without dragging its heels once and will keep the reader glued to every sexy page.<br />The author adeptly twists and turns and uses every trick in her book to make the reader's heart flutter, sigh, cry and scream with delight in this delectable offering.<br />So what are you waiting for. Go read it now!<br />A FIVE STAR romantic novel and highly recommended. </span>

<div id="review_710496729" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/710496729" />
    <a title="Alex Rosa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13717591-alex-rosa"><img alt="Alex Rosa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587842058p2/13717591.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/710496729?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex Rosa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex Rosa" href="/user/show/13717591-alex-rosa">Alex Rosa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710496729" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6591242934160564525">Oh, where to start with this book. I adore this author anyways, and was excited to delve into her first published work! I was not disappointed. I don't read rock star type romances often, but must confess I secretly love them.<br/> <br/>This book was curious from the start and I honestly was unsure how I would feel about it. I could not deny that Jack Storm and Marissa Duplei's first steamy encounter in the first chapter pulled me in, but when suddenly a chapter or two later, (and 5 years in story time) t</span>
  <span id="freeText6591242934160564525" style="display:none">Oh, where to start with this book. I adore this author anyways, and was excited to delve into her first published work! I was not disappointed. I don't read rock star type romances often, but must confess I secretly love them.<br /> <br />This book was curious from the start and I honestly was unsure how I would feel about it. I could not deny that Jack Storm and Marissa Duplei's first steamy encounter in the first chapter pulled me in, but when suddenly a chapter or two later, (and 5 years in story time) there is a child involved I was like -woah! How do I feel about this? My personal preference when reading romance is I am not a fan of pregnancy, and such, but Lisa Gillis has me turning over a new leaf. I loved the adorable Tristan! Who's perfect mixture of unavoidable childlike persona, and surprisingly adorable adult understanding was just so wonderful. Not to mention his interactions with his "momma" and "new friend" Jack.<br /> <br />I enjoyed the main character Marissa who never wilted, or faltered in her struggles but was strong from the beginning to end. I like that ... a lot! She had her frantic moments, but she still felt so solid. Even when she met Jack Storm, to dealing with her pregnancy, and being a fantastic Mom, and also a wonderful match for her rock star infatuation ;) Though, her constant dieting habits had me squirming. Marissa would be mentioning calorie counts in ice cream WHILE I WAS EATING ICE CREAM AND READING ...none the less, I still just wished it was Jack Storm bringing me a pint ;)<br /> <br />Jack Storm, I wanted more of him, but this is a good thing! He intrigued me from the start, and all I ever wanted was to get inside his had, and maybe his pants *shrugs* haha. I was surprised to find him so kind and caring. But my most favorite part was his calculated observing. He seemed to do everything with purpose, even when he didn't necessarily know what to do.<br /> <br />I loved Jack and Marissa’s interactions. A moment never seemed wasted and I felt like I was stumbling through it all with them. Jack seemed like an enigma from the start, but I really fell for the fact that Marissa felt connected to him all that time, even if she was truly just starting to get to know him. Not only did they have to get to know each other, but they had to come together as parents. Finding the balance did not come easy, and defenses were up on both ends while mixing that with their intense attraction to one another. The journey as a reader was fun to be apart of! Their steamy scenes weren’t lacking either, and I have to admit I could have had a bit more. Haha.<br /> <br />Now, last, but definitely not least. I absolutely adored Jack insistence with getting to know his son and wanting to be involved. I don’t know how the author did it but his supreme confidence, and open vulnerability with getting used to the idea of being a father was just *swoon* wonderful.<br /> <br />I really loved this book from start to finish, and I cannot wait to get my hands on book 2 “Weathering Jack Storm”, which is available now. Now, go read this book now! You won’t be disappointed! 5 out of 5!<br /><br />(read other book reviews on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.authorarosa.com">www.authorarosa.com</a>)</span>
  <a data-text-id="6591242934160564525" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer843732396" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10547180898371865814"><strong>REFRESHING!</strong><br/><br/><br/>This was such a refreshing story! I fell hard and fast for Jack. With some of the things he said, you can't help but to love him. <br/><br/>"I don't know why l say the shit I do sometimes. I don't know that guy either. Unfortunately, I have to live with his screw ups. I don't want you to be one of those things I screwed up."<br/><br/>And:<br/><br/>"I'm asking with you want to get married one day. Because I know I want to marry you. But we need to build a relationship. And, your proposal should be spectacular. So t</span>
  <span id="freeText10547180898371865814" style="display:none"><strong>REFRESHING!</strong><br /><br /><br />This was such a refreshing story! I fell hard and fast for Jack. With some of the things he said, you can't help but to love him. <br /><br />"I don't know why l say the shit I do sometimes. I don't know that guy either. Unfortunately, I have to live with his screw ups. I don't want you to be one of those things I screwed up."<br /><br />And:<br /><br />"I'm asking with you want to get married one day. Because I know I want to marry you. But we need to build a relationship. And, your proposal should be spectacular. So this is not it."<br /><br />Don't that just make you swoon!<br /><br />Lisa Gillis has a refreshing writing style. It didn't take me long to find the rhythm of this book. They were times when I thought she was going back and forth between first and third person, but I was never once confused. One more of my reading hick ups, or maybe her writing is just that strong. I'm not sure. I just know is that I love this book.<br /><br />"The kiss he laid on her was caring, tender, and forgiving, and the kiss she gave back was convincing, trusting, and fiery with love."<br /><br />I liked how she let the emotions play out. They both were on shaky ground. Neither one sure of how the other was feeling you see and feel their suspicions and their hopes. <br /><br />If it wasn't for my tired eyes, I would have finished this book in one setting. As it was, it took me about three hours to finish book one, but that's three hours I didn't have for book two. Now that I know there's a book three, well, y'all know what I'm doing for the next few days. Take care...<br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText4061049142193874093" style="display:none">"Jack Who? (Silver Strings Series G)" by Lisa Gillia is a great romantic read about a rock star and 'regular' woman.<br />Meeting under unusual circumstances the two have a one night stand but they loose touch. Years later they have business to sort out between them.<br />The complexities of fame, the real person behind a rockstar image and the possibility of true love are themes that Gillis plays out well in this enjoyable and fast paced story.The book is an easy read and has some great characters, an all round winner for fans of the genre. </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16184714524242534692">The perfect fix for the craving I was having for a good rockstar romance! Imminently more satisfying than the first one I chose last night. I am looking forward to delving further into this series in the very near future.<br/><br/>To me, this one pretty well has it all. Gorgeous rocker stud, sweet, insecure young girl. Ooops, the hookup led to a pregnancy and letting him know is not what she thinks he would want to hear. Fast forward 5 years and her little reminder of her romp on the wildside is in need o</span>
  <span id="freeText16184714524242534692" style="display:none">The perfect fix for the craving I was having for a good rockstar romance! Imminently more satisfying than the first one I chose last night. I am looking forward to delving further into this series in the very near future.<br /><br />To me, this one pretty well has it all. Gorgeous rocker stud, sweet, insecure young girl. Ooops, the hookup led to a pregnancy and letting him know is not what she thinks he would want to hear. Fast forward 5 years and her little reminder of her romp on the wildside is in need of expensive surgery and she finally decides it is time for him to know he can add "Daddy" to his guitar strap. Her love for her son, her insecurities, her fantasies about her famous one night stand are all so real and powerful. The author does a fantastic job of portraying all of Marissa's emotions.<br /><br />Yes, it is all wrapped up eventually in a HEA situation, and what a fun ride it is to get there. If you can't fall in love with Tristan, you have no heart. This is just an oh so sweet story all the way around. Lighter on the smut than I would usually seek in this type of story, but I got so wrapped up in the entire plot that it didn't bother me in the slightest.<br /><br />I am so excited to know that this is a series and already more are available. I can't extend this review any longer because I am anxious to move onto the next one.</span>

  <span id="freeText3167942099222764681" style="display:none">Jack Who? kept me up all night! I just downloaded this literary gem yesterday. I only meant to read a few pages to get the flavor of the story and ended up devouring the whole thing. This rockin’ romance was an easy read that drew me in from the first word and locked me in until the last. It takes a ton of hard work and talent to tell a story this smoothly and seamlessly. Throw in a cast of colorful characters, a thrilling hero, a relatable heroine, intense desire, palpable attraction and just the right amount of conflict, and you have a blissful reading experience. Jack Who? is a romance readers dream come true! By the way, this was my first rock star romance, but it won’t be my last. I’m off to buy the rest of the books in this series right now!</span>

Marissa might be in the middle of a thought and that reminds her of another thought, or the doorbell rings or her son needs to get out of the tub. 5 stars for putting the real in rockstar</span>
  <span id="freeText3982131250839552755" style="display:none">What i like about this book is that it is real, complete with kid being a kid and a dog to trip over. I LOVE the real dialogue. These two interrupt each others sentences in a fight, they trail off as they are trying to say something but can't find the words. And the same with the scenes. So much like real life. Marissa might be in the middle of a thought and that reminds her of another thought, or the doorbell rings or her son needs to get out of the tub. 5 stars for putting the real in rockstar Lisa Gillis! </span>
  <a data-text-id="3982131250839552755" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1945266591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12800593168000408654">Super read for anyone young at heart!<br/><br/>Wonderful characters and a real sense of adventure captured in this easy read romance. I loved the determination of Marissa not to get caught up in the rock star life style. <br/><br/>My only complaint is that I now have to go and buy the rest of the books in this fab series! Completely hooked! </span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13217999173191515800" style="display:none">Review in Portuguese and English.<br /><br />blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bookwhorebr.blogspot.com.br/2013/11/jack-who-silver-strings-g-1-by-lisa.html">http://bookwhorebr.blogspot.com.br/20...</a><br /><br />Marissa acaba de terminar o namoro com um cara que a estava traindo com outra mulher. Aliás ela pega os dois no ato.<br />Ela sai com uma amiga para se divertir e também curar o coração partido dela.<br />As duas vão a um concerto de rock onde várias bandas irão se apresentar. Ela vai mais para acompanhar a amiga, pois ela nem curte este estilo musical.<br />A amiga dela a Olivia a deixa sozinha e vai atrás de um dos ídolos dela.<br />Marissa acha um cachorro perdido e vai em busca do dono do bichinho.<br />Ela conhece Jack, mas ela não sabe que ele é o astro de uma das bandas de rock.<br />Os dois tem umas horas de sexo incrível e cada um segue seu caminho.<br />Alguns meses depois ela recebe um telefonema de Jack, mas ela não vai ao encontro dele.<br />A história pula 5 anos no tempo...<br />Após todo este tempo Marissa é obrigada a contactar Jack. O filho deles está com um grave problema de saúde e ela precisa da ajuda dele.<br />Quando ele recebe o telefonema dela ele fica furioso e manda ela lidar diretamente com os advogados dele. Ele não acredita que o filho é dele.<br />Marissa engole o próprio orgulho e aceita as exigências dos advogados, afinal a saúde do filho está em jogo.<br />No dia da cirurgia Jack aparece no hospital e ela fica surpresa com o apoio que ele oferece pra ela.<br />A partir dali os dois começam a forjar um relacionamento que é abalado pela fama dele, pela publicitária que cuida da imagem da banda, pela família de ambos e todo tipo de interferência externa que acontece na vida de uma celebridade.<br />Marissa sofre todo tipo de pressão ao tentar se ajustar à vida de Jack. E ainda por cima a irmã dele desconfia que o filho não é dele e exige um exame de DNA.<br />Nós vamos acompanhando uma série de acontecimentos e acabamos duvidando que o casal consiga se ajustar.<br />Ciúmes, dúvidas, imprensa, empregados... tudo conspira para a falência do relacionamento deles.<br />Mas os dois se amam e é muito legal acompanhar o relacionamento dos dois.<br />O amor de Jack pelo filho também é muito lindo, os dois se conectam desde o primeiro instante.<br />O livro não tem final e continua no próximo volume.<br /><br />-------------------------------<br /><br />Marissa has just break up with a guy who was cheating on her with another woman. In fact she picks up the two in the Act.<br />She goes out with a friend to have fun and also heal the broken heart.<br />The two go to a rock concert where various bands will perform. She goes over to accompany her friend because she doesn't enjoy this musical style.<br />Her friend Olivia leaves her alone and go after one of her idols.<br />Marissa finds a stray dog and goes in search of the owner of the pet.<br />She meets Jack, but she doesn't know that he's the star of one of the rock bands.<br />Both have a few hours of great sex and each go our separate ways.<br />A few months later she receives a call from Jack, but she's not going to meet him.<br />The story jumps 5 years in time.<br />After all this time Marissa is obliged to contact Jack. Their son is with a serious health problem and she needs his help.<br />When he receives the call from her he gets mad and says she deal directly with his lawyers. He doesn't believe the child is his.<br />Marissa swallows his pride and accept the demands of the lawyers, after all the child's health is at stake.<br />On the day of surgery Jack appears in the hospital and she is surprised with the support he provides for her.<br />From there the two begin to forge a relationship that is shaken by his fame, the publicist who takes care of the band's image, by both family and all sorts of external interference that happens in the life of a celebrity.<br />Marissa suffers all kinds of pressure when trying to fit the life of Jack. And on top of his sister suspects that the child is not his and require a DNA test.<br />We will follow a series of events and just doubting that the couple can adjust.<br />Jealousy, doubt, press, employees ... everything conspires to the bankruptcy of their relationship.<br />But the two are in love and it's very nice to follow the relationship of the two.<br />Jack's love for his son is also very beautiful, both connect from the first moment.<br />The book has no end and continues in the next volume.<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_804648393" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/804648393" />
    <a title="Merrie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15180557-merrie"><img alt="Merrie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1375235823p2/15180557.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/804648393?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Merrie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Merrie" href="/user/show/15180557-merrie">Merrie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25632540-jack-who">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15180557-merrie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15180557-merrie?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15180557-merrie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15180557-merrie?shelf=rock-star">rock-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer804648393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15327609423122236257">I remember when I first read this book back in October 2013 and I fell in love with it. So, when I decided to give it a re-read, I was a little worried that it wasn't going to be as good as I remembered. Needless to say, it was just as good, if not better than I remembered. I do really enjoy the Rock Star genre and this series is pretty high up on my favorites list.<br/><br/>This book will be told through the third person POV of Marissa, our female lead.<br/><br/>The beginning of Jack Who? finds our female lead, Ma</span>
  <span id="freeText15327609423122236257" style="display:none">I remember when I first read this book back in October 2013 and I fell in love with it. So, when I decided to give it a re-read, I was a little worried that it wasn't going to be as good as I remembered. Needless to say, it was just as good, if not better than I remembered. I do really enjoy the Rock Star genre and this series is pretty high up on my favorites list.<br /><br />This book will be told through the third person POV of Marissa, our female lead.<br /><br />The beginning of Jack Who? finds our female lead, Marissa, and her BFF, Olivia, at a rock festival. This isn't really Marissa's speed, but Olivia is dying to get backstage so she can meet some rock gods. Somehow Marissa and Olivia get separated and instead of Marissa searching for the debauchery that Olivia is sure to find, she comes across a dog. Yes, a dog. The owner of the dog is no other than Jack Storm, the lead singer for Jackal. I should go ahead and point out that while the world may know who Jack Storm and Jackal is, Marissa does not fall into that particular category.<br /><br />Let's cut to the good stuff. Once in Jack's trailer, quips get exchanged, consent form gets signed, and sex gets had. One would think that this is just a one time thing, but they do exchange phone numbers, however, several months down the road and Marissa finds herself expecting a child, Jack's child to be exact. In her mind it is best to not say a word to her baby daddy and when he texts her and asks her to fly out to L.A. to visit, she kinda has to give him the ole' blow off, which pisses Jack off and in turn, cutting off all contact between the two. <br /><br />Fast forward 5 years and she is left with no choice but to make an attempt to contact Jack. Their son, Tristan, is in need of surgery and Marissa is in need of money. After some back and forth, surgery day has arrived and so has Jack, much to the shock of Marissa. Well, really to the shock of everyone, because Marissa never disclosed the identity of Tristan's father, not even to Olivia.<br /><br />Even though their was an order for Marissa to get a DNA test, once Jack lays eyes on Tristan, he knows without a doubt that he is now a father. At this point, the majority of the remainder of the book is really focusing on Jack and Tristan developing a relationship as well as, Marissa and Jack trying to rekindle what they felt between them five years earlier.<br /><br />There are so many great things about this book, where to begin? First, is Tristan. He is so wonderfully written. He is witty, funny, smart, and not at all hindered by his disability. Then of course, there is his relationship with those around him. He is very inviting to Jack and vice versa. I mean, it can't be an easy day when you meet your son that you didn't know about for five years, but he handles it very well. And while you know that Jack is a rock star, his only focus is really getting to know his son and Marissa. <br /><br />The supporting cast of characters here are really, really in the background here and this is one time that I am perfectly okay with it. I think that this is one of those storylines that needs to put all of the energy into the main characters. That's not to say that there isn't any focus on the secondary cast, there is, it's just not in your face.<br /><br />What would a Rock Star romance be like without discussing the sex? The sex that is written is spicy enough, but like the supporting characters, it isn't one of the focal points of Jack Who?, it is part of it though, and I do wish there was a little bit more sinning. Having said that, the times that Marissa and Jack tangle up, it is in rock star fashion.<br /><br />This is a pretty quick read, it's only 266 pages and it will certainly captivate you and keep the pages turning. I have read the next two books in this series and as a whole, this is a fantastic series. Like I said, it is one of my favorite Rock Star series and if this is your genre, even if it's not, give it a go.<br /><br />For more reviews, visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bxtchesbeblogging.com">www.bxtchesbeblogging.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15327609423122236257" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Women throw themselves at him, toss their lingerie on the stage, and scream his name. Marissa has no idea of his public identity, and while she does not initially throw herself at him, she does go on to toss aside her lingerie and ultimately scream his name.<br><br>Five minutes after parting, Marissa holds no illusions about seeing him again, but does vow a new outlook on her life and herself.<br><br>Five days later, they exchange a very short text.<br><br>Five months later, Jack astounds her with an invitation to Los Angeles. Although Jack is now a star in her very non rock star fantasies, Marissa is concealing a huge secret that prevents her from accepting.<br><br>Five years later, the secret comes out and despite the conflicting emotions each feels towards the another, they must meld their two worlds together.<br><p>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1918393849" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4258360740982464210">Rockin' Romance.<br/><br/>Author Lisa Gillis knows how to write romance. This story revolves around Marissa, a woman who caught her boyfriend cheating on her, and Jack, a sexy musician.<br/><br/>Marissa wants revenge against her boyfriend and is looking for a hookup. She encounters Jack, and she gets much more than she expected.<br/><br/>I enjoyed the characters and the situations the author put them in. The book was a pleasure to read, and I look forward to enjoying more books by this talented writer.<br/><br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12736289072848445886" style="display:none">Ok where do I want to start. I laughed and cried through out the book. I will say that I felt connected to the characters and even in Jack Storm I see my husband who can be a pain the a$$. <br /><br />It starts off with Marissa's best friend getting her in backstage at a music fest which does not lie on how they get back stage. Then a dog comes running up to her and she does not see the owner so she goes looking. Now she meets the hot guy and does not have a clue who he is but a metal star. She takes her best friends advice and uses him to get over her cheating ex-fiancee. <br /><br />The book then joins ahead 5 months when they are talking on the phone and her misgivings about meeting him. <br /><br />The book then jumps ahead 5 years. She has to reach out to get help with the surgery really needed for her son that he does not know anything about.<br /><br />There is a lot of drama. I like how even though they share a son they take time to learn each other. <br /><br />Four stars is because of the childish behaviors that happen in the book. There was parts that I felt like both characters needed to grow up because the child was acting more mature then they were. Enjoy the book because I did.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Kaf1QFfYj8zhwpEEub4NFRus0bN3OIOCsFmcUiEyVK7/WYqo1oIoovxyM83nvoNhfWJUx4PraUu+nFLrz+LE4w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
